<div class="wp-block-stackable-columns alignfull stk-block-columns stk-block stk-d0bf6a6 stk-block-background" data-block-id="d0bf6a6"><div class="stk-row stk-inner-blocks stk-block-content stk-content-align stk-d0bf6a6-column alignfull">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk-block stk-f52bc02 champagnetext" data-v="4" data-block-id="f52bc02"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-f52bc02-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk--column-flex stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-f52bc02-inner-blocks">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-heading stk-block-heading stk-block-heading--v2 stk-block stk-93df83d" id="welcome-to-rachel-irl" data-block-id="93df83d"><h1 class="stk-block-heading__text has-text-color has-text-align-center">Welcome to Rachel IRL!</h1></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-ef67a60 champagnetext" data-block-id="ef67a60"><p class="stk-block-text__text has-text-color">After 10+ years of travel trial and error, I’ve gotten really good at having <strong>real life travel experiences</strong> that feel like mine.</p></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-19c5e4e champagnetext" data-block-id="19c5e4e"><p class="stk-block-text__text has-text-color">This blog will empower you to have <strong>travel</strong> <strong>experiences that feel uniquely yours</strong>, based on <strong>what <em>actually</em> makes you happy.</strong>&nbsp;We’re de-prioritizing the top 10 things to do according to your old guidebook &amp; re-prioritizing what <em><strong>you</strong></em> want to do.</p></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-288c1e3 champagnetext" data-block-id="288c1e3"><p class="stk-block-text__text has-text-color">I’ll encourage you to <strong>plug in</strong> to the rhythm of any place, <strong>appreciate</strong> different ways of life, and <strong>adapt</strong> to new cultures in a way that’s energizing and respectful.</p></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-6173938 champagnetext" data-block-id="6173938"><p class="stk-block-text__text has-text-color">What you’ll find here are my<strong> real experiences</strong> in places I’ve loved, and my <strong>true opinions </strong>about every destination.</p></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-50aac05 champagnetext" data-block-id="50aac05"><p class="stk-block-text__text has-text-color">Happy to have you here!</p></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-button-group stk-block-button-group stk-block stk-b1e0846" data-block-id="b1e0846"><div class="stk-row stk-inner-blocks has-text-align-center stk-block-content stk-button-group">

<!-- Fix popup dismissal (we hope) -->
<script type="rocketlazyloadscript">
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
  function forciblyClosePopup() {
    const popup = document.querySelector('.adp-popup');
    const overlay = document.querySelector('.adp-popup-overlay');
    if (popup) {
      popup.style.display = 'none';
      popup.classList.remove('popupOpenSlide');
      popup.classList.add('popupExitSlide');
    }
    if (overlay) {
      overlay.style.display = 'none';
    }
    document.body.classList.remove('adp-popup-scroll-hidden');
  }

  // Hijack clicks anywhere inside the popup's close button or overlay
  document.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
    if (
      e.target.closest('.adp-popup-close') ||
      e.target.classList.contains('adp-popup-overlay')
    ) {
      e.preventDefault();
      forciblyClosePopup();
    }
  });

  // ESC key fallback
  document.addEventListener('keydown', function (e) {
    if (e.key === 'Escape') {
      forciblyClosePopup();
    }
  });
});
</script>
